   430	
   431	                info = Constants.IV_INFO;
   432	                var iv = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   433	
   434	                return AesGcmDecrypt(ciphertextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   435	            }
   436	            catch (Exception error)
   437	            {

   440	            }

   443	        /// <summary>
   444	        /// HPKE-Base mode encrypt (P-256 / HKDF-SHA256 / AES-128-GCM).
   445	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>crypto.ts hpkeEncrypt</c>.
   446	        /// </summary>
   447	        /// <returns>
   448	        /// The byte concatenation
   449	        /// <c>compressed(senderPub) || ciphertext</c>, ready to feed to
   450	        /// <see cref="FormatHpkeBuf"/> or <see cref="DecryptCredentialBundle"/>.
   451	        /// </returns>
   452	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">
   453	        /// Wraps any underlying failure with the upstream message
   454	        /// <c>"Unable to perform hpkeEncrypt: ..."</c>.
   455	        /// </exception>
   456	        public static byte[] HpkeEncrypt(HpkeEncryptParams parameters)
   457	        {
   458	            try
   459	            {
   460	                if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   461	                var plainTextBuf = parameters.PlainTextBuf
   462	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.PlainTextBuf));
   463	                var targetKeyBuf = parameters.TargetKeyBuf
   464	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.TargetKeyBuf));
   465	
   466	                var ephemeralKeyPair = GenerateP256KeyPair();
   467	                var senderPrivBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.PrivateKey);
   468	                var senderPubBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   469	
   470	                var aad = BuildAdditionalAssociatedData(senderPubBuf, targetKeyBuf);
   830	                {
   831	                    throw new InvalidOperationException("missing \"encappedPublic\" in bundle signed data");
   832	                }
   833	                string? ciphertextStr = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "ciphertext");
   834	
   835	                var encappedKeyBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(encappedPublic!);
   836	                var ciphertextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ciphertextStr!);
   837	
   838	                var decryptedData = HpkeDecrypt(new HpkeDecryptParams
   839	                {
   840	                    CiphertextBuf = ciphertextBuf,
   841	                    EncappedKeyBuf = encappedKeyBuf,
   842	                    ReceiverPriv = parameters.EmbeddedKey,
   843	                });
   844	
   845	                if (string.Equals(parameters.KeyFormat, "SOLANA", StringComparison.Ordinal)
   846	                    && !parameters.ReturnMnemonic)
   847	                {
   848	                    if (decryptedData.Length != 32)
   849	                    {
   850	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   851	                            "invalid private key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + decryptedData.Length + ".");
   852	                    }
   853	                    // Derive Ed25519 public key from the 32-byte seed via BouncyCastle.
   854	                    var ed25519PrivKey = new Ed25519PrivateKeyParameters(decryptedData, 0);
   855	                    var publicKeyBytes = ed25519PrivKey.GeneratePublicKey().GetEncoded();
   856	                    if (publicKeyBytes.Length != 32)
   857	                    {
   858	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   859	                            "invalid public key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + publicKeyBytes.Length + ".");
   860	                    }
   861	                    var concatenated = new byte[64];
   862	                    Array.Copy(decryptedData, 0, concatenated, 0, 32);
   863	                    Array.Copy(publicKeyBytes, 0, concatenated, 32, 32);
   864	                    return Encoding.Base58Encode(concatenated);
   865	                }
   866	
   867	                var decryptedHex = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(decryptedData);
   868	                return parameters.ReturnMnemonic ? Encoding.HexToAscii(decryptedHex) : decryptedHex;
   869	            }
   870	            catch (Exception error)

     1	import { p256 } from "@noble/curves/p256";
     2	import { createHash } from "sha256-uint8array";
     3	import { uint8ArrayToHexString } from "@turnkey/encoding";
     4	
     5	export const signWithApiKey = async (input: {
     6	  content: string;
     7	  publicKey: string;
     8	  privateKey: string;
     9	}): Promise<string> => {
    10	  const publicKey = p256.getPublicKey(input.privateKey, true);
    11	
    12	  // Public key in the usual 02 or 03 + 64 hex digits
    13	  const publicKeyString = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey);
    14	
    15	  if (publicKeyString != input.publicKey) {
    16	    throw new Error(
    17	      `Bad API key. Expected to get public key ${input.publicKey}, got ${publicKeyString}`,
    18	    );
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  const hash = createHash().update(input.content).digest();
    22	  const signature = p256.sign(hash, input.privateKey);
    23	  return signature.toDERHex();
    24	};

     1	/// <reference lib="dom" />
     2	import { stringToBase64urlString } from "@turnkey/encoding";
     3	
     4	// Header name for an API key stamp
     5	const stampHeaderName = "X-Stamp";
     6	
     7	export type Runtime = "browser" | "node" | "purejs";
     8	
     9	export type TApiKeyStamperConfig = {
    10	  apiPublicKey: string;
    11	  apiPrivateKey: string;
    12	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined;
    13	};
    14	
    15	// `window.document` ensures that we're in a browser context
    16	// and `crypto.subtle` ensures that it supports the web crypto APIs
    17	// Inspired by https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    18	const isCryptoEnabledBrowser: boolean =
    19	  typeof window !== "undefined" &&
    20	  typeof window.document !== "undefined" &&
    21	  typeof crypto !== "undefined" &&
    22	  typeof crypto.subtle !== "undefined";
    23	
    24	// We check `process.versions.node`
    25	// Taken from https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    26	const isNode: boolean =
    27	  typeof process !== "undefined" &&
    28	  process.versions != null &&
    29	  process.versions.node != null;
    30	
    31	const detectRuntime = (): Runtime => {
    32	  if (isCryptoEnabledBrowser) {
    33	    return "browser";
    34	  }
    35	
    36	  if (isNode) {
    37	    return "node";
    38	  }
    39	
    40	  // If we don't have NodeJS or web crypto at our disposal, default to pure JS implementation
    41	  // This is the case for old browsers and react native environments
    42	  return "purejs";
    43	};
    44	
    45	/**
    46	 * Signature function abstracting the differences between NodeJS and web environments for signing with API keys.
    47	 */
    48	export const signWithApiKey = async (
    49	  input: {
    50	    content: string;
    51	    publicKey: string;
    52	    privateKey: string;
    53	  },
    54	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined,
    55	): Promise<string> => {
    56	  const runtime = runtimeOverride ?? detectRuntime();
    57	
    58	  switch (runtime) {
    59	    case "browser":
    60	      return (await import("./webcrypto")).signWithApiKey(input);
    61	    case "node":
    62	      return (await import("./nodecrypto")).signWithApiKey(input);
    63	    case "purejs":
    64	      return (await import("./purejs")).signWithApiKey(input);
    65	    default:
    66	      throw new Error(`Unsupported runtime: ${runtime}`);
    67	  }
    68	};
    69	
    70	/**
    71	 * Stamper to use with `@turnkey/http`'s `TurnkeyClient`
    72	 */
    73	export class ApiKeyStamper {
    74	  apiPublicKey: string;
    75	  apiPrivateKey: string;
    76	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined;
    77	
    78	  constructor(config: TApiKeyStamperConfig) {
    79	    this.apiPublicKey = config.apiPublicKey;
    80	    this.apiPrivateKey = config.apiPrivateKey;
    81	    this.runtimeOverride = config.runtimeOverride;
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  async stamp(payload: string) {
    85	    const signature = await signWithApiKey(
    86	      {
    87	        publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    88	        privateKey: this.apiPrivateKey,
    89	        content: payload,
    90	      },
    91	      this.runtimeOverride,
    92	    );
    93	
    94	    const stamp = {
    95	      publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    96	      scheme: "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256",
    97	      signature,
    98	    };
    99	
   100	    return {
   101	      stampHeaderName,
   102	      stampHeaderValue: stringToBase64urlString(JSON.stringify(stamp)),
   103	    };
   104	  }
   105	}

    20	  { impl: signPureJS, name: "sign (PureJS)" },
    21	  { impl: signUniversal, name: "sign (universal)" },
    22	])("sign with Turnkey fixture: $name", async ({ impl: sign }) => {
    23	  const { privateKey, publicKey, pemPublicKey } = await readFixture();
    24

    26

    28	    content,
    29	    privateKey,

    31	  });
    32	
    33	  // We can't snapshot `actualStamp.signature` because P-256 signatures are not deterministic
    34	  expect(

    36	      content,
    37	      pemPublicKey,

    39	    }),
    40	  ).toBe(true);

    48	    });
    49	  }).toThrow();

    31	  test("hpkeAuthEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - end-to-end encryption and decryption", () => {
    32	    const senderKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    33	    const receiverKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    34	    const receiverPublicKeyUncompressed = uncompressRawPublicKey(
    35	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverKeyPair.publicKey),
    36	    );
    37	
    38	    const textEncoder = new TextEncoder();

    40	    const plainText = "Hello, this is a secure message!";
    41	    const plainTextBuf = textEncoder.encode(plainText);
    42	    // Encrypt

    44	      plainTextBuf: plainTextBuf,
    45	      targetKeyBuf: receiverPublicKeyUncompressed,
    46	      senderPriv: senderKeyPair.privateKey,
    47	    });
    48	    const encryptedData = formatHpkeBuf(encryptedDataBuf);
    49	    // Extract the encapsulated key buffer and the ciphertext

    51	    // Decrypt
    52	    const decryptedData = hpkeDecrypt({
    53	      ciphertextBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.ciphertext),
    54	      encappedKeyBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.encappedPublic),
    55	      receiverPriv: receiverKeyPair.privateKey,
    56	    });
    57	
    58	    // Convert decrypted data back to string
    59	    const decryptedText = new TextDecoder().decode(decryptedData);
    60	
    61	    // Expect the decrypted text to equal the original plaintext
    62	    expect(decryptedText).toEqual(plainText);
    63	  });

    66	describe("HPKE Standard Encryption and Decryption", () => {
    67	  test("hpkeEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - standard mode (ephemeral sender key)", async () => {
    68	    // Generate a receiver key pair
    69	    const receiverKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    70	    const receiverPublicKeyUncompressed = uncompressRawPublicKey(
    71	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverKeyPair.publicKey),
    72	    );

    74	    // Prepare the plaintext

    76	    const plainText =
    77	      "6ab33bd6e4bdc73017233da0554f9616fe10ede5c3ce001e81b321d5a74199b7";
    78	    const plainTextBuf = textEncoder.encode(plainText);

    81	    const encryptedDataBuf = hpkeEncrypt({
    82	      plainTextBuf: plainTextBuf,
    83	      targetKeyBuf: receiverPublicKeyUncompressed,
    84	      // No senderPriv provided, so it will use an ephemeral key
    85	    });

    87	    // Parse the encrypted data
    88	    const data = JSON.parse(encryptedData);

    91	      ciphertextBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.ciphertext),
    92	      encappedKeyBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.encappedPublic),
    93	      receiverPriv: receiverKeyPair.privateKey,
    94	    });
    95	
    96	    // Convert decrypted data back to string
    97	    const decryptedText = new TextDecoder().decode(decryptedData);
    98	
    99	    // Verify that the decrypted text matches the original plaintext

   115	      "enclaveQuorumPublic": "04cf288fe433cc4e1aa0ce1632feac4ea26bf2f5a09dcfe5a42c398e06898710330f0572882f4dbdf0f5304b8fc8703acd69adca9a4bbf7f5d00d20a5e364b2569"
   116	    }
   117	  `;
   118	  const privateKey =
   119	    "ffc6090f14bcf260e5dfe63f45412e60a477bb905956d7cc90195b71c2a544b3";
   120	  const organizationId = "f9a31c64-d604-42e4-9bef-a773096afad7";

   169	    expect(keyPair.publicKey).not.toEqual(keyPair.publicKeyUncompressed);

   199	  test("verifyRequestStamp", async () => {
   200	    const { publicKey: apiPublicKey, privateKey: apiPrivateKey } =
   201	      generateP256KeyPair();
   202	    const apiKeyStamper = new ApiKeyStamper({
   203	      apiPublicKey,
   204	      apiPrivateKey,
   205	    });
   206	
   207	    const turnkeyClient = new TurnkeyClient(
   208	      {
   209	        baseUrl: "https://api.turnkey.com",
   210	      },
   211	      apiKeyStamper,
   212	    );
   213	
   214	    const stampedRequest = await turnkeyClient.stampGetWhoami({
   215	      organizationId: "00000000-00000000-00000000-00000000",
   216	    });
   217	
   218	    const stampContents = stampedRequest.stamp.stampHeaderValue;
   219	    const decodedStampContents = atob(stampContents);
   220	    const parsedStampContents = JSON.parse(decodedStampContents);
   221	    const signature = parsedStampContents.signature;
   222	
   223	    const verified = await verifyStampSignature(
   224	      apiPublicKey,
   225	      signature,
   226	      stampedRequest.body,
   227	    );
   228	
   229	    expect(verified).toEqual(true);
   230	  });

   261	
   262	  describe("Valid DER signatures", () => {
   263	    test("should parse a simple DER signature with short-form length", () => {
   264	      // Create a signature with 32-byte r and s values
   265	      const rValue = new Array(32).fill(0x01);
   266	      const sValue = new Array(32).fill(0x02);
   267	      const totalLength = 2 + 32 + 2 + 32; // 2 bytes for each INTEGER header + values
   268	
   269	      const derHex = createDerSignature([totalLength], rValue, sValue);
   270	
   271	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   272	    });
   273	
   274	    test("should parse a DER signature with 33-byte integers (with leading zero)", () => {
   275	      // ECDSA signatures sometimes have leading zeros to ensure positive integers
   276	      const rValue = [0x00, ...new Array(32).fill(0x80)]; // Leading zero + high bit set
   277	      const sValue = [0x00, ...new Array(32).fill(0x90)];
   278	      const totalLength = 2 + 33 + 2 + 33;
   279	
   280	      const derHex = createDerSignature([totalLength], rValue, sValue);
   281	
   282	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   283	    });
   284	  });
   285	
   286	  describe("Invalid signatures - missing SEQUENCE tag", () => {
   287	    test("should reject signatures without SEQUENCE tag (0x30)", () => {
   288	      const invalidHex = bytesToHex([
   289	        0x31, // Wrong tag (should be 0x30)
   290	        0x44, // Length of SEQUENCE
   291	        0x02,
   292	        0x20,
   293	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   294	        0x02,
   295	        0x20,
   296	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   297	      ]);
   298	
   299	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidHex)).toThrow(
   300	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid format (missing SEQUENCE tag)",
   301	      );
   302	    });
   303	
   304	    test("should reject empty signatures", () => {
   305	      expect(() => fromDerSignature("")).toThrow(
   306	        "cannot create uint8array from invalid hex string",
   307	      );
   308	    });
   309	
   310	    test("should reject signatures that are too short", () => {
   311	      const shortHex = bytesToHex([0x30]); // Only SEQUENCE tag, no length
   312	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(shortHex)).toThrow(
   313	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: insufficient length",
   314	      );
   315	    });
   316	  });
   317	
   318	  describe("Invalid signatures - length field issues", () => {
   319	    test("should reject signatures with unsupported length encoding (0x80-0xFE range)", () => {
   320	      const unsupportedLengthHex = bytesToHex([
   321	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   322	        0x81, // Length encoding value that we do not want to support
   323	        0x44, // Length value
   324	        // ... rest of signature would follow
   325	      ]);
   326	
   327	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(unsupportedLengthHex)).toThrow(
   328	        /large or invalid signature length/,
   329	      );
   330	    });
   331	
   332	    test("should handle edge case of maximum short-form length (0x7F)", () => {
   333	      // This would be a very large signature chunk with trailing data, but valid short-form
   334	      const rValue = new Array(32).fill(0x01);
   335	      const sValue = new Array(32).fill(0x02);
   336	
   337	      const derHex = bytesToHex([
   338	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   339	        0x7f, // Maximum short-form length of SEQUENCE
   340	        0x02, // INTEGER tag
   341	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   342	        ...rValue, // r (34 bytes total for INTEGER including header)
   343	        0x02, // INTEGER tag
   344	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   345	        ...sValue, // s (34 bytes total for INTEGER including header)
   346	        ...new Array(0x7f - 68).fill(0x00), // Padding to reach 0x7F total length
   347	      ]);
   348	
   349	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   350	    });
   351	
   352	    test("should reject signatures with invalid r length", () => {
   353	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   354	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   355	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   356	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   357	        0x22, // length of INTEGER // invalid -- should be 32 or 33
   358	        ...new Array(34).fill(0x01), // r
   359	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   360	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   361	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   362	      ]);
   363	
   364	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   365	        /unexpected length for r/,
   366	      );
   367	    });
   368	
   369	    test("should reject signatures with invalid s length", () => {
   370	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   371	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   372	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   373	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   374	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   375	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   376	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   377	        0x22, // length of INTEGER // invalid -- should be 32 or 33
   378	        ...new Array(34).fill(0x02), // s
   379	      ]);
   380	
   381	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   382	        /unexpected length for s/,
   383	      );
   384	    });
   385	
   386	    test("should reject signatures with invalid, non-padding r bytes", () => {
   387	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   388	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   389	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   390	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   391	        0x21, // length of INTEGER // 33 -- this is valid
   392	        ...new Array(33).fill(0x01), // r -- this is invalid, as the first byte in a 33 byte sequence is a non-padding byte
   393	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   394	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   395	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   396	      ]);
   397	
   398	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   399	        /invalid number of starting zeroes/,
   400	      );
   401	    });
   402	
   403	    test("should reject signatures with invalid, non-padding s bytes", () => {
   404	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   405	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   406	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   407	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   408	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   409	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   410	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   411	        0x21, // length of INTEGER // 33 -- this is valid
   412	        ...new Array(33).fill(0x02), // s -- this is invalid, as the first byte in a 33 byte sequence is a non-padding byte
   413	      ]);
   414	
   415	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   416	        /invalid number of starting zeroes/,
   417	      );
   418	    });
   419	  });
   420	
   421	  describe("Invalid signatures - INTEGER parsing", () => {
   422	    test("should reject signatures with invalid r INTEGER tag", () => {
   423	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   424	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   425	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   426	        0x03, // WRONG tag for r (0x03 instead of 0x02)
   427	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   428	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   429	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   430	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   431	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   432	      ]);
   433	
   434	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   435	        /invalid tag for r/,
   436	      );
   437	    });
   438	
   439	    test("should reject signatures with invalid s INTEGER tag", () => {
   440	      const invalidSTagHex = bytesToHex([
   441	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   442	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   443	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   444	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   445	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   446	        0x03, // WRONG tag for s (0x03 instead of 0x02)
   447	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   448	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   449	      ]);
   450	
   451	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidSTagHex)).toThrow(
   452	        /invalid tag for s/,
   453	      );
   454	    });
   455	  });
   456	});

   460	    const jwt =

   469	
   470	// Helper function to create hex strings from byte arrays
   471	const bytesToHex = (bytes: number[]): string => {
   472	  return bytes.map((b) => b.toString(16).padStart(2, "0")).join("");
   473	};
   474	
   475	// Helper function to create a basic DER signature structure
   476	const createDerSignature = (
   477	  sequenceLength: number[],
   478	  rValue: number[],
   479	  sValue: number[],
   480	): string => {

 succeeded in 0ms:
   760	            }
   761	
   762	            string? targetPublic = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "targetPublic");
   763	            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(targetPublic))
   764	            {
   765	                throw new InvalidOperationException("missing \"targetPublic\" in bundle signed data");
   766	            }
   767	
   768	            var targetKeyBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(targetPublic!);
   769	            var privateKeyBundle = HpkeEncrypt(new HpkeEncryptParams
   770	            {
   771	                PlainTextBuf = plainTextBuf,
   772	                TargetKeyBuf = targetKeyBuf,
   773	            });
   774	            return FormatHpkeBuf(privateKeyBundle);
   775	        }
   776	
   777	        /// <summary>
   778	        /// Decrypt a Turnkey export bundle.
   779	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>turnkey.ts decryptExportBundle</c>.
   780	        /// </summary>
   781	        public static string DecryptExportBundle(DecryptExportBundleParams parameters)
   782	        {
   783	            if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   784	            if (parameters.ExportBundle == null)
   785	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.ExportBundle));
   786	
   787	            // Upstream order, exactly:
   788	            //   1. enter try
   789	            //   2. JSON.parse(exportBundle)
   790	            //   3. verifyEnclaveSignature(...)
   791	            //   4. parse signed data, check organizationId, encappedPublic
   792	            //   5. hpkeDecrypt
   793	            //   6. format output (SOLANA / mnemonic / hex)
   794	            //   catch -> "Error decrypting bundle: ..."
   795	            try
   796	            {
   797	                using var bundleDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(parameters.ExportBundle);
   798	                var parsedExportBundle = bundleDoc.RootElement;
   799	
   800	                string? enclaveQuorumPublic = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "enclaveQuorumPublic");
   801	                string? dataSignature = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "dataSignature");
   802	                string? dataHex = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "data");
   803	
   804	                bool verified = VerifyEnclaveSignature(
   805	                    enclaveQuorumPublic,
   806	                    dataSignature,
   807	                    dataHex,
   808	                    parameters.DangerouslyOverrideSignerPublicKey);
   809	                if (!verified)
   810	                {
   811	                    throw new InvalidOperationException(
   812	                        "failed to verify enclave signature: " + parameters.ExportBundle);
   813	                }
   814	
   815	                var signedDataBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(dataHex!);
   816	                using var signedDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(signedDataBytes));
   817	                var signedData = signedDoc.RootElement;
   818	
   819	                string? bundleOrgId = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "organizationId");
   820	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(bundleOrgId)
   821	                    || !string.Equals(bundleOrgId, parameters.OrganizationId, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   822	                {
   823	                    throw new InvalidOperationException(
   824	                        "organization id does not match expected value. Expected: " + parameters.OrganizationId
   825	                        + ". Found: " + bundleOrgId + ".");
   826	                }
   827	
   828	                string? encappedPublic = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "encappedPublic");
   829	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(encappedPublic))
   830	                {
   831	                    throw new InvalidOperationException("missing \"encappedPublic\" in bundle signed data");
   832	                }
   833	                string? ciphertextStr = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "ciphertext");
   834	
   835	                var encappedKeyBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(encappedPublic!);
   836	                var ciphertextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ciphertextStr!);
   837	
   838	                var decryptedData = HpkeDecrypt(new HpkeDecryptParams
   839	                {
   840	                    CiphertextBuf = ciphertextBuf,
   841	                    EncappedKeyBuf = encappedKeyBuf,
   842	                    ReceiverPriv = parameters.EmbeddedKey,
   843	                });
   844	
   845	                if (string.Equals(parameters.KeyFormat, "SOLANA", StringComparison.Ordinal)
   846	                    && !parameters.ReturnMnemonic)
   847	                {
   848	                    if (decryptedData.Length != 32)
   849	                    {
   850	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   851	                            "invalid private key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + decryptedData.Length + ".");
   852	                    }
   853	                    // Derive Ed25519 public key from the 32-byte seed via BouncyCastle.
   854	                    var ed25519PrivKey = new Ed25519PrivateKeyParameters(decryptedData, 0);
   855	                    var publicKeyBytes = ed25519PrivKey.GeneratePublicKey().GetEncoded();
   856	                    if (publicKeyBytes.Length != 32)
   857	                    {
   858	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   859	                            "invalid public key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + publicKeyBytes.Length + ".");
   860	                    }
   861	                    var concatenated = new byte[64];
   862	                    Array.Copy(decryptedData, 0, concatenated, 0, 32);
   863	                    Array.Copy(publicKeyBytes, 0, concatenated, 32, 32);
   864	                    return Encoding.Base58Encode(concatenated);
   865	                }
   866	
   867	                var decryptedHex = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(decryptedData);
   868	                return parameters.ReturnMnemonic ? Encoding.HexToAscii(decryptedHex) : decryptedHex;
   869	            }
   870	            catch (Exception error)
   871	            {
   872	                throw new InvalidOperationException(
   873	                    "Error decrypting bundle: " + error.Message, error);
   874	            }
   875	        }
   876	
   877	        /// <summary>
   878	        /// Verify the ECDSA signature on a Turnkey session JWT.
   879	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>turnkey.ts verifySessionJwtSignature</c>.
   880	        /// </summary>
   881	        /// <param name="jwt">The JWT to verify.</param>
   882	        /// <param name="dangerouslyOverrideNotarizerPublicKey">
   883	        /// Optional hex-encoded uncompressed P-256 public key to verify
   884	        /// against. Use for tests only; defaults to the production
   885	        /// notarizer key.
   886	        /// </param>
   887	        /// <returns><c>true</c> if the signature is valid for the given key.</returns>
   888	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">Thrown when the JWT is malformed (missing parts).</exception>
   889	        public static bool VerifySessionJwtSignature(
   890	            string jwt,
   891	            string? dangerouslyOverrideNotarizerPublicKey = null)
   892	        {
   893	            if (jwt == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(jwt));
   894	
   895	            string notarizerKeyHex =
   896	                dangerouslyOverrideNotarizerPublicKey ?? Constants.PRODUCTION_NOTARIZER_SIGN_PUBLIC_KEY;
   897	
   898	            var parts = jwt.Split('.');
   899	            // Upstream: const [a, b, sig] = jwt.split("."); if (!sig) throw new Error(...)
   900	            if (parts.Length < 3 || string.IsNullOrEmpty(parts[2]))
   901	            {
   902	                throw new InvalidOperationException("invalid JWT: need 3 parts");
   903	            }
   904	
   905	            string headerB64 = parts[0];
   906	            string payloadB64 = parts[1];
   907	            string signatureB64 = parts[2];
   908	            string signingInput = headerB64 + "." + payloadB64;
   909	
   910	            byte[] msgDigest;
   911	            using (var sha256 = SHA256.Create())
   912	            {
   913	                var h1 = sha256.ComputeHash(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(signingInput));
   914	                msgDigest = sha256.ComputeHash(h1);
   915	            }
   916	
   917	            byte[] signature = Base64UrlDecode(signatureB64);
   918	            var publicKey = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(notarizerKeyHex);
   919	            return VerifyP256RawSignature(publicKey, signature, msgDigest);
   920	        }
   921	
   922	        #endregion
   923	
   924	        #region Private helpers
   925	
   926	        private static byte[] DeriveSS(byte[] encappedKeyBuf, string privHex)
   927	        {
   928	            // Upstream noble p256.getSharedSecret validates the private scalar.
   929	            var privBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(privHex);
   930	            var (d, domainParams) = ValidateAndDeserializeP256PrivateKey(privBytes);
  1020	            int len = cipher.ProcessBytes(encryptedData, 0, encryptedData.Length, output, 0);
  1021	            cipher.DoFinal(output, len);
  1022	            return output;
  1023	        }
  1024	
  1025	        private static byte[] AesGcmEncrypt(byte[] plainData, byte[] key, byte[] iv, byte[] aad)
  1026	        {
  1027	            var cipher = new GcmBlockCipher(new AesEngine());
  1028	            cipher.Init(true, new AeadParameters(new KeyParameter(key), 128, iv, aad));
  1029	
  1030	            var output = new byte[cipher.GetOutputSize(plainData.Length)];
  1031	            int len = cipher.ProcessBytes(plainData, 0, plainData.Length, output, 0);
  1032	            cipher.DoFinal(output, len);
  1033	            return output;
  1034	        }
  1035	
  1036	        private static byte[] Base64UrlDecode(string input)
  1037	        {
  1038	            var output = input.Replace('-', '+').Replace('_', '/');
  1039	            switch (output.Length % 4)
  1040	            {
  1041	                case 2: output += "=="; break;
  1042	                case 3: output += "="; break;
  1043	            }
  1044	            return Convert.FromBase64String(output);
  1045	        }
  1046	
  1047	        private static bool VerifyP256RawSignature(byte[] publicKeyBytes, byte[] signatureRaw, byte[] messageDigest)
  1048	        {
  1049	            // Upstream noble p256.verify accepts r||s of length 64. Anything
  1050	            // else is an invalid signature; return false.
  1051	            if (signatureRaw.Length != 64)
  1052	            {
  1053	                return false;
  1054	            }
  1055	            try
  1056	            {
  1057	                var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
  1058	                var domainParams = new ECDomainParameters(curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
  1059	
  1060	                var point = curve.Curve.DecodePoint(publicKeyBytes);
  1061	                var publicKeyParams = new ECPublicKeyParameters(point, domainParams);
  1062	
  1063	                var r = new BigInteger(1, signatureRaw, 0, 32);
  1064	                var s = new BigInteger(1, signatureRaw, 32, 32);
  1065	                byte[] derSignature = new DerSequence(new DerInteger(r), new DerInteger(s)).GetDerEncoded();
  1066	
  1067	                var signer = SignerUtilities.GetSigner("NONEwithECDSA");
  1068	                signer.Init(false, publicKeyParams);
  1069	                signer.BlockUpdate(messageDigest, 0, messageDigest.Length);
  1070	                return signer.VerifySignature(derSignature);
  1071	            }
  1072	            catch
  1073	            {
  1074	                return false;
  1075	            }
  1076	        }
  1077	
  1078	        /// <summary>
  1079	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>turnkey.ts verifyEnclaveSignature</c>.
  1080	        /// Returns <c>true</c> when the signature verifies, <c>false</c>
  1081	        /// when the underlying ECDSA verify fails. Throws on mismatched
  1082	        /// signer key (matches upstream "expected signer key ... does not
  1083	        /// match signer key from bundle").
  1084	        /// </summary>
  1085	        private static bool VerifyEnclaveSignature(

     8	# but never two different runs in parallel for the same tag.
     9	concurrency:
    10	  group: release-${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    11	  cancel-in-progress: false

    18	
    19	jobs:
    20	  publish:
    21	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    22	    env:
    23	      RELEASE_TAG:      ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    24	      GITHUB_ACTOR_ENV: ${{ github.actor }}
    25	
    26	    steps:
    27	      # actions/checkout v6.0.2 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
    28	      - name: Checkout tag
    29	        uses: actions/checkout@de0fac2e4500dabe0009e67214ff5f5447ce83dd
    30	        with:
    31	          ref: ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    32	          fetch-depth: 0
    33	          # Drop checkout token from .git/config after checkout — later
    34	          # git/gh calls pass `GH_TOKEN` explicitly and never authenticate
    35	          # via the persisted checkout credential, so persisting it
    36	          # extends the token's blast radius without benefit.
    37	          persist-credentials: false
    38	
    39	      - name: Parse + validate strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag
    40	        id: ver
    41	        env:
    42	          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
    43	        run: |
    44	          set -euo pipefail
    45	          # Strict SemVer 2.0.0 (no build metadata): vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]
    46	          # PRERELEASE = identifier (. identifier)*
    47	          # identifier = numeric (no leading zero) | alphanumeric
    48	          re='^v(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)(-((0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*)(\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*))*))?$'
    49	          if [[ ! "$TAG" =~ $re ]]; then
    50	            echo "::error::Tag '$TAG' is not strict SemVer 2.0.0 (vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]; no build metadata)."
    51	            exit 1
    52	          fi
    53	          echo "version=${TAG#v}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    54	          echo "tag=$TAG"          >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    55	
    56	      - name: Resolve tag commit SHA
    57	        id: tagsha
    58	        env:
    59	          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
    60	        run: |
    61	          set -euo pipefail
    62	          echo "sha=$(git rev-parse "${TAG}^{commit}")" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    63	
    64	      - name: Verify tag commit is contained in main
    65	        env:
    66	          GH_TOKEN:   ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    67	          OWNER_REPO: ${{ github.repository }}
    68	          TAG_SHA:    ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
    69	        run: |
    70	          set -euo pipefail
    71	          # Use the REST compare API instead of `git fetch origin main`.
    72	          # Reason: `actions/checkout` ran with `persist-credentials:
    73	          # false` (security), so the runner's `.git/config` has no
    74	          # credential to authenticate a `git fetch` against this
    75	          # private repo. `gh api` reads `GH_TOKEN` from the env and
    76	          # works against private repos without persisting a git
    77	          # credential.
    78	          #
    79	          # Semantics: GET /repos/{repo}/compare/{base}...{head} returns
    80	          # `status` ∈ {ahead, behind, identical, diverged}, where
    81	          # `base = main` and `head = TAG_SHA`. The tag is reachable
    82	          # from main iff main contains the tag commit, i.e. main has
    83	          # commits the tag does not (status: `behind`) or main and
    84	          # tag point to the same commit (status: `identical`). Any
    85	          # other status (`ahead`, `diverged`) means the tag carries
    86	          # commits not on main and must be rejected.
    87	          STATUS=$(gh api "repos/${OWNER_REPO}/compare/main...${TAG_SHA}" --jq .status)
    88	          case "$STATUS" in
    89	            behind|identical)
    90	              echo "tag ${TAG_SHA} reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS})"
    91	              ;;
    92	            *)
    93	              echo "::error::Tag commit ${TAG_SHA} is not reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS}). Releases must be cut from a commit on main."
    94	              exit 1
    95	              ;;
    96	          esac
    97

    99	      - name: Setup .NET 8
   100	        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@c2fa09f4bde5ebb9d1777cf28262a3eb3db3ced7
   101	        with:
   102	          dotnet-version: 8.0.x

   201	      - name: Preflight existing Release assets (unconditional)
   202	        id: preflight
   203	        env:
   204	          GH_TOKEN:        ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   205	          TAG:             ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
   206	          VERSION:         ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   207	          NUPKG_SHA256:    ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
   208	          SNUPKG_SHA256:   ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_sha256 }}
   209	          NUPKG_PATH:      ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
   210	          SNUPKG_PATH:     ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_path }}
   211	          CHECKSUMS_PATH:  ${{ steps.checksums.outputs.checksums_path }}
   212	          NUPKG_NAME:      KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.nupkg
   213	          SNUPKG_NAME:     KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.snupkg
   214	        run: |
   215	          set -euo pipefail
   216	          mkdir -p ./_release_assets
   217	          HAS_PRIOR=false
   218	
   219	          # Enumerate assets that actually exist on the Release. We do NOT
   220	          # treat a failed `gh release download` as "asset missing" —
   221	          # that would swallow auth / rate-limit / API errors. Instead
   222	          # query `gh release view` first and download only what is
   223	          # present.
   224	          assets_json=$(gh release view "$TAG" --json assets)
   225	          present() {
   226	            local name="$1"
   227	            jq -e --arg n "$name" '.assets[] | select(.name == $n)' >/dev/null \
   228	              <<< "$assets_json"
   229	          }
   230	
   231	          # If an asset is present, download MUST succeed; failure here
   232	          # is a hard error (closed-fail).
   233	          check_one() {
   234	            local name="$1"
   235	            local sha256="$2"
   236	            if ! present "$name"; then
   237	              echo "preflight: $name absent"
   238	              return 0
   239	            fi
   240	            HAS_PRIOR=true
   241	            if ! gh release download "$TAG" \
   242	                 --pattern "$name" --dir ./_release_assets; then
   243	              echo "::error::Asset '$name' is listed on the Release but download failed."
   244	              exit 1
   245	            fi
   246	            local existing
   247	            existing=$(sha256sum "./_release_assets/$name" | awk '{print $1}')
   248	            if [[ "$existing" != "$sha256" ]]; then
   249	              echo "::error::Existing Release asset $name sha256 ($existing) differs from local ($sha256). Refusing to clobber."
   250	              exit 1
   251	            fi
   252	            echo "preflight: $name byte-equal"

   567	/**
   568	 * Encrypt data using AES-GCM.

   570	const aesGcmEncrypt = (
   571	  plainTextData: Uint8Array,
   572	  key: Uint8Array,

   595	/**
   596	 * Generate a Key Encapsulation Mechanism (KEM) context.
   597	 */
   598	const getKemContext = (
   599	  encappedKeyBuf: Uint8Array,
   600	  publicKey: string,
   601	): Uint8Array => {
   602	  const encappedKeyArray = new Uint8Array(encappedKeyBuf);
   603	  const publicKeyArray = uint8ArrayFromHexString(publicKey);
   604	
   605	  const kemContext = new Uint8Array(
   606	    encappedKeyArray.length + publicKeyArray.length,
   607	  );
   608	  kemContext.set(encappedKeyArray);
   609	  kemContext.set(publicKeyArray, encappedKeyArray.length);
   610	
   611	  return kemContext;
   612	};
   613	
   614	/**
   615	 * Convert a BigInt to a hexadecimal string of a specific length.
   616	 */
   617	const bigIntToHex = (num: bigint, length: number): string => {
   618	  const hexString = num.toString(16);
   619	  if (hexString.length > length) {
   620	    throw new Error(
   621	      `number cannot fit in a hex string of ${length} characters`,
   622	    );
   623	  }
   624	  return hexString.padStart(length, "0");
   625	};
   626	
   627	/**
   628	 * Converts an ASN.1 DER-encoded ECDSA signature to the raw format used for verification.
   629	 *
   630	 * @param {string} derSignature - The DER-encoded signature.
   631	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The raw signature.
   632	 */
   633	export const fromDerSignature = (derSignature: string): Uint8Array => {
   634	  const derSignatureBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(derSignature);
   635	
   636	  // Check minimum length
   637	  if (derSignatureBuf.length < 2) {
   638	    throw new Error(
   639	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: insufficient length",
   640	    );
   641	  }
   642	
   643	  // Check SEQUENCE tag (0x30 at first byte)
   644	  if (derSignatureBuf[0] !== 0x30) {
   645	    throw new Error(
   646	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid format (missing SEQUENCE tag)",
   647	    );
   648	  }
   649	
   650	  // Check second byte, start of length field
   651	  let index = 1;
   652	  const lengthByte = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   653	  if (lengthByte <= 0x7f) {
   654	    // Short form: single byte length
   655	
   656	    // directly take the consumed value as length and check against buffer
   657	    // buffer length: initial header bytes + claimed remaining length
   658	    if (derSignatureBuf.length < 1 + 1 + lengthByte) {
   659	      throw new Error(
   660	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: inconsistent message length header",
   661	      );
   662	    }
   663	
   664	    // continue parsing
   665	    index += 1;
   666	  } else {
   667	    // Multi-byte DER length header
   668	    // Invalid DER values: lengthByte 0x80 and 0xff
   669	    // Valid DER values: lengthByte > 0x80, < 0xff
   670	    //
   671	    // We do not expect signature data in the Long form notation
   672	    // -> reject all such inputs
   673	    //
   674	    // More complex parsing for longer signature sequences can be implemented once needed
   675	    throw new Error(
   676	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpectedly large or invalid signature length",
   677	    );
   678	  }
   679	
   680	  // Parse 'r' and check for integer tag (0x02)
   681	  if (derSignatureBuf[index] !== 0x02) {
   682	    throw new Error(
   683	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid tag for r",
   684	    );
   685	  }
   686	
   687	  index++; // Move past the INTEGER tag
   688	  const rLength = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   689	
   690	  // Allow up to 32 data bytes + 1 byte 0-padding prefix
   691	  if (rLength > 33) {
   692	    throw new Error(
   693	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpected length for r",
   694	    );
   695	  }
   696	
   697	  index++; // Move past the length byte
   698	  const r = derSignatureBuf.slice(index, index + rLength);
   699	  index += rLength; // Move to the start of s
   700	
   701	  // Parse 's' and check for integer tag (0x02)
   702	  if (derSignatureBuf[index] !== 0x02) {
   703	    throw new Error(
   704	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid tag for s",
   705	    );
   706	  }
   707	
   708	  index++; // Move past the INTEGER tag
   709	  const sLength = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   710	
   711	  // Allow up to 32 data bytes + 1 byte 0-padding prefix
   712	  if (sLength > 33) {
   713	    throw new Error(
   714	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpected length for s",
   715	    );
   716	  }
   717	
   718	  index++; // Move past the length byte
   719	  const s = derSignatureBuf.slice(index, index + sLength);
   720	
   721	  // Normalize 'r' and 's' to 32 bytes each
   722	  const rPadded = normalizePadding(r, 32);
   723	  const sPadded = normalizePadding(s, 32);
   724	
   725	  // Concatenate and return the raw signature
   726	  return new Uint8Array([...rPadded, ...sPadded]);
   727	};
   728	
   729	/**
   730	 * Converts a raw ECDSA signature to DER-encoded format.
   731	 *
   732	 * This function takes a raw ECDSA signature, which is a concatenation of two 32-byte integers (r and s),
   733	 * and converts it into the DER-encoded format. DER (Distinguished Encoding Rules) is a binary encoding
   734	 * for data structures described by ASN.1.
   735	 *
   736	 * @param {string} rawSignature - The raw signature in hexadecimal string format.
   737	 * @returns {string} - The DER-encoded signature in hexadecimal string format.
   738	 *
   739	 * @throws {Error} - Throws an error if the input signature is invalid or if the encoding process fails.
   740	 *
   741	 * @example
   742	 * // Example usage:
   743	 * const rawSignature = "0x487cdb8a88f2f4044b701cbb116075c4cabe5fe4657a6358b395c0aab70694db3453a8057e442bd1aff0ecabe8a82c831f0edd7f2158b7c1feb3de9b1f20309b1c";
   744	 * const derSignature = toDerSignature(rawSignature);
   745	 * console.log(derSignature); // Outputs the DER-encoded signature as a hex string
   746	 * // "30440220487cdb8a88f2f4044b701cbb116075c4cabe5fe4657a6358b395c0aab70694db02203453a8057e442bd1aff0ecabe8a82c831f0edd7f2158b7c1feb3de9b1f20309b"
   747	 */
   748	export const toDerSignature = (rawSignature: string) => {
   749	  const rawSignatureBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(rawSignature);
   750	
   751	  // Split raw signature into r and s, each 32 bytes
   752	  const r = rawSignatureBuf.slice(0, 32);
   753	  const s = rawSignatureBuf.slice(32, 64);
   754	
   755	  // Helper function to encode an integer with DER structure
   756	  const encodeDerInteger = (integer?: Uint8Array): Uint8Array => {
   757	    // Check if integer is defined and has at least one byte
   758	    if (
   759	      integer === undefined ||
   760	      integer.length === 0 ||
   761	      integer[0] === undefined
   762	    ) {
   763	      throw new Error("Invalid integer: input is undefined or empty.");
   764	    }
   765	
   766	    // Add a leading zero if the integer's most significant byte is >= 0x80
   767	    const needsPadding = integer[0] & 0x80;
   768	    const paddedInteger = needsPadding
   769	      ? new Uint8Array([0x00, ...integer])
   770	      : integer;
   771	
   772	    // Prepend the integer tag (0x02) and length
   773	    return new Uint8Array([0x02, paddedInteger.length, ...paddedInteger]);
   774	  };
   775	
   776	  // DER encode r and s
   777	  const rEncoded = encodeDerInteger(r);
   778	  const sEncoded = encodeDerInteger(s);
   779	
   780	  // Combine as a DER sequence: 0x30, total length, rEncoded, sEncoded
   781	  const derSignature = new Uint8Array([
   782	    0x30,
   783	    rEncoded.length + sEncoded.length,
   784	    ...rEncoded,
   785	    ...sEncoded,
   786	  ]);
   787	
   788	  return uint8ArrayToHexString(derSignature);
   789	};
   790	
   791	/**
   792	 * Create a shared AES-GCM secret with the quorum key encryption SHA-512 HMAC
   793	 *
   794	 * This function takes an ephemeral Sender public key generated for each encryption operation
   795	 * the corresponding ephemeral private key, and the target public key uncompressed
   796	 * for data structures described by ASN.1.
   797	 *
   798	 * @param {Uint8Array} ephemeralSenderPublic - The ephemeral public key used to create the preImage
   799	 * @param {Uint8Array} ephemeralSenderPrivate - The ephemeral private key to create the shared secret with
   800	 * @param {Uint8Array} targetPublicKeyUncompressed - The public key to create the shared secret with and encrypt the message to
   801	 * @returns {Promise<CryptoKey>} - A shared secret AES-GCM key between ephemeralSenderPrivate and the targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   802	 */
   803	async function createQuorumKeyEncryptCipher(
   804	  ephemeralSenderPublic: Uint8Array,
   805	  ephemeralSenderPrivate: Uint8Array,
   806	  targetPublicKeyUncompressed: Uint8Array,
   807	): Promise<CryptoKey> {
   808	  // create the shared secret between ephemeralSenderPrivate and targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   809	  const sharedSecretUncompressed = p256.getSharedSecret(
   810	    ephemeralSenderPrivate,
   811	    targetPublicKeyUncompressed,
   812	    false,
   813	  );
   814	  const sharedSecret = sharedSecretUncompressed.slice(1, 33);
   815	
   816	  // create the preImage as defined in qos here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L273-L282
   817	  let preImage = new Uint8Array(
   818	    ephemeralSenderPublic.length +
   819	      targetPublicKeyUncompressed.length +
   820	      sharedSecret.length,
   821	  );
   822	  preImage.set(ephemeralSenderPublic, 0);
   823	  preImage.set(targetPublicKeyUncompressed, ephemeralSenderPublic.length);
   824	  preImage.set(
   825	    sharedSecret,
   826	    ephemeralSenderPublic.length + targetPublicKeyUncompressed.length,
   827	  );
   828	
   829	  // create the HMAC key and create an HMAC using QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE
   830	  const hmacKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
   831	    "raw",
   832	    preImage,
   833	    {
   834	      name: "HMAC",
   835	      hash: "SHA-512",
   836	    },
   837	    false,
   838	    ["sign"],
   839	  );
   840	  const mac = new Uint8Array(
   841	    await crypto.subtle.sign("HMAC", hmacKey, QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE),
   842	  );
   843	
   844	  // Use the first 32 bytes as the AES-GCM key
   845	  const aesKeyRaw = mac.slice(0, 32);
   846	
   847	  return crypto.subtle.importKey(
   848	    "raw",
   849	    aesKeyRaw,
   850	    {
   851	      name: "AES-GCM",
   852	    },
   853	    false,
   854	    ["encrypt"],
   855	  );
   856	}

   858	/// Helper function to create the additional associated data (AAD). The data is
   859	/// of the form `sender_public||sender_public_len||receiver_public||receiver_public_len`.
   860	/// This is taken from QOS here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L298

     1	import {
     2	  uint8ArrayFromHexString,
     3	  uint8ArrayToHexString,
     4	} from "@turnkey/encoding";

     7	import { sha256 } from "@noble/hashes/sha2";
     8	import * as CBOR from "cbor-js";
     9	import * as x509 from "@peculiar/x509";
    10	import { AWS_ROOT_CERT_PEM, AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256 } from "./constants";
    11	
    12	export const getCryptoInstance = async () => {
    13	  let cryptoInstance: Crypto;
    14	  // Use globalThis.crypto.subtle if available
    15	  if (typeof globalThis !== "undefined" && globalThis.crypto?.subtle) {
    16	    cryptoInstance = globalThis.crypto as Crypto;
    17	    x509.cryptoProvider.set(cryptoInstance);
    18	
    19	    return cryptoInstance;
    20	  } else {
    21	    throw new Error(
    22	      "Web Crypto API is not available in this environment. You may need to polyfill it.",
    23	    );
    24	  }
    25	};
    26	
    27	/**
    28	 * Utility: SHA-256 digest → hex (uppercase)
    29	 */
    30	async function sha256Hex(data: Uint8Array): Promise<string> {
    31	  const cryptoInstance = await getCryptoInstance();
    32	  const digest = await cryptoInstance.subtle.digest("SHA-256", data);
    33	  return uint8ArrayToHexString(new Uint8Array(digest)).toUpperCase();
    34	}
    35	
    36	/**
    37	 * Utility: Import SPKI public key for ECDSA verify
    38	 */
    39	async function importEcdsaPublicKey(spki: ArrayBuffer): Promise<CryptoKey> {
    40	  const cryptoInstance = await getCryptoInstance();
    41	  return cryptoInstance.subtle.importKey(
    42	    "spki",
    43	    spki,
    44	    { name: "ECDSA", namedCurve: "P-384" }, // AWS Nitro uses ES384
    45	    false,
    46	    ["verify"],
    47	  );
    48	}
    49	
    50	/**
    51	 * verify goes through the following verification steps for an app proof & boot proof pair:
    52	 *  - Verify app proof signature
    53	 *  - Verify the boot proof
    54	 *    - Attestation doc was signed by AWS
    55	 *    - Attestation doc's `user_data` is the hash of the qos manifest
    56	 *  - Verify the connection between the app proof & boot proof i.e. that the ephemeral keys match
    57	 *
    58	 *  For more information, check out https://whitepaper.turnkey.com/foundations
    59	 */
    60	export async function verify(
    61	  appProof: v1AppProof,
    62	  bootProof: v1BootProof,
    63	): Promise<void> {
    64	  // 1. Verify App Proof
    65	  verifyAppProofSignature(appProof);
    66	
    67	  // 2. Verify Boot Proof
    68	  // Parse attestation
    69	  const coseSign1Der = Uint8Array.from(
    70	    atob(bootProof.awsAttestationDocB64)
    71	      .split("")
    72	      .map((c) => c.charCodeAt(0)),
    73	  );
    74	  const coseSign1 = CBOR.decode(coseSign1Der.buffer);
    75	  const [, , payload] = coseSign1;
    76	  const attestationDoc = CBOR.decode(new Uint8Array(payload).buffer);
    77	
    78	  // Verify cose sign1 signature
    79	  await verifyCoseSign1Sig(coseSign1, attestationDoc.certificate);
    80	
    81	  // Verify certificate chain
    82	  const appProofTimestampMs = parseInt(
    83	    JSON.parse(appProof.proofPayload).timestampMs,
    84	  );
    85	  await verifyCertificateChain(
    86	    attestationDoc.cabundle,
    87	    AWS_ROOT_CERT_PEM,
    88	    attestationDoc.certificate,
    89	    appProofTimestampMs,
    90	  );
    91	
    92	  // Verify manifest digest
    93	  const decodedBootProofManifest = Uint8Array.from(
    94	    atob(bootProof.qosManifestB64)
    95	      .split("")
    96	      .map((c) => c.charCodeAt(0)),
    97	  );
    98	  const manifestDigest = sha256(decodedBootProofManifest);
    99	  if (!bytesEq(manifestDigest, attestationDoc.user_data)) {
   100	    throw new Error(
   101	      `attestationDoc's user_data doesn't match the hash of the manifest. attestationDoc.user_data: ${attestationDoc.user_data} , manifest digest: ${manifestDigest}`,
   102	    );
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  // 3. Verify that all the ephemeral public keys match: app proof, boot proof structure, actual attestation doc
   106	  const publicKeyBytes = new Uint8Array(attestationDoc.public_key);
   107	  const attestationPubKey = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKeyBytes);
   108	  if (
   109	    appProof.publicKey !== attestationPubKey ||
   110	    attestationPubKey !== bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex
   111	  ) {
   112	    throw new Error(
   113	      `Ephemeral pub keys from app proof: ${appProof.publicKey}, boot proof structure ${bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex}, and attestation doc ${attestationPubKey} should all match`,
   114	    );
   115	  }
   116	}
   117	
   118	/**
   119	 * Verify app proof signature with @noble/curves
   120	 */
   121	export function verifyAppProofSignature(appProof: v1AppProof): void {
   122	  if (appProof.scheme !== "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_EPHEMERAL_KEY_P256") {
   123	    throw new Error("Unsupported signature scheme");
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  // Decode public key
   127	  let publicKeyBytes: Uint8Array;
   128	  try {
   129	    publicKeyBytes = uint8ArrayFromHexString(appProof.publicKey);
   130	  } catch {
   131	    throw new Error("Failed to decode public key");
   132	  }
   133	
   134	  if (publicKeyBytes.length !== 130) {
   135	    throw new Error(
   136	      `Expected 130 bytes (encryption + signing pub keys), got ${publicKeyBytes.length} bytes`,
   137	    );
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  // Extract signing key (last 65 bytes, uncompressed P-256 point)
   141	  const signingKeyBytes = publicKeyBytes.slice(65);
   142	  if (signingKeyBytes.length !== 65 || signingKeyBytes[0] !== 0x04) {
   143	    throw new Error(
   144	      "Invalid signing key format: expected 65-byte uncompressed P-256 point (0x04||X||Y)",
   145	    );
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  // Validate it's a valid P-256 public key by attempting to create a point
   149	  try {
   150	    p256.ProjectivePoint.fromHex(signingKeyBytes);
   151	  } catch (error) {
   152	    throw new Error(`Invalid P-256 public key: ${error}`);
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  // Decode signature (64 bytes = 32 bytes r + 32 bytes s)
   156	  let signatureBytes: Uint8Array;
   157	  try {
   158	    signatureBytes = uint8ArrayFromHexString(appProof.signature);
   159	  } catch {
   160	    throw new Error("Failed to decode signature");
   161	  }
   162	  if (signatureBytes.length !== 64) {
   163	    throw new Error(
   164	      `Expected 64 bytes signature (r||s), got ${signatureBytes.length} bytes`,
   165	    );
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  // Hash the proof payload
   169	  const payloadBytes = new TextEncoder().encode(appProof.proofPayload);
   170	  const payloadDigest = sha256(payloadBytes);
   171	
   172	  // Verify ECDSA signature
   173	  const isValid = p256.verify(signatureBytes, payloadDigest, signingKeyBytes);
   174	  if (!isValid) {
   175	    throw new Error("Signature verification failed");
   176	  }
   177	}
   178	
   179	export async function verifyCertificateChain(
   180	  cabundle: Uint8Array[],
   181	  rootCertPem: string,
   182	  leafCert: Uint8Array,
   183	  timestampMs: number,
   184	): Promise<void> {
   185	  try {
   186	    // Check root and assert fingerprint
   187	    const rootX509 = new x509.X509Certificate(rootCertPem);
   188	    const rootDer = new Uint8Array(rootX509.rawData);
   189	    const rootSha = await sha256Hex(rootDer);
   190	    if (rootSha !== AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256) {
   191	      throw new Error(
   192	        `Pinned AWS root fingerprint mismatch: expected=${AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256} actual=${rootSha}`,
   193	      );
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    // Bundle starts with root certificate. We're replacing the root with our hardcoded known certificate, so remove first element
   197	    const bundleWithoutRoot = cabundle.slice(1);
   198	    const intermediatesX509 = bundleWithoutRoot.map((c) => {
   199	      if (!c) throw new Error("Invalid certificate data in cabundle");
   200	      return new x509.X509Certificate(c);
   201	    });
   202	    const leaf = new x509.X509Certificate(leafCert);
   203	
   204	    // Build path leaf → intermediates → root, with our hardcoded known root certificate
   205	    const builder = new x509.X509ChainBuilder({
   206	      certificates: [rootX509, ...intermediatesX509],
   207	    });
   208	    const chain = await builder.build(leaf);
   209	    if (chain.length !== intermediatesX509.length + 2) {
   210	      throw new Error(
   211	        `Incorrect number of certs in X509 Chain. Expected ${intermediatesX509.length + 2}, got ${chain.length}`,
   212	      );
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    const appProofDate = new Date(timestampMs);
   216	    for (let i = 0; i < chain.length; i++) {
   217	      const cert = chain[i];
   218	      if (!cert) throw new Error("Invalid certificate in chain");
   219	
   220	      if (i === chain.length - 1) {
   221	        // is root
   222	        // Self-signature verification for root certificate
   223	        const ok = await cert.verify({
   224	          publicKey: cert.publicKey,
   225	          date: appProofDate,
   226	        });
   227	        if (!ok)
   228	          throw new Error("Pinned root failed self-signature verification");
   229	      } else {
   230	        // Verify signature against issuer
   231	        const issuer = chain[i + 1];
   232	        if (!issuer) throw new Error("Issuer can't be null");
   233	
   234	        // Attestation docs technically expire after 3 hours, so an app proof generated 3+ hours after an enclave
   235	        // boots up will fail verification due to certificate expiration. This is okay because enclaves are immutable;
   236	        // even if the cert is technically invalid, the code contained within it cannot change. To prevent the cert
   237	        // expiration failure, we set `signatureOnly: true`.
   238	        const ok = await cert.verify({
   239	          publicKey: issuer.publicKey,
   240	          signatureOnly: true,

exec

   241	          date: appProofDate,
   242	        });
   243	        if (!ok) {
   244	          throw new Error(
   245	            `Signature check failed: ${cert.subject} not signed by ${issuer?.subject}`,
   246	          );
   247	        }
   248	      }
   249	    }
   250	  } catch (error) {
   251	    throw new Error(
   252	      `Certificate chain verification failed: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)}`,
   253	    );
   254	  }
   255	}
   256	
   257	export async function verifyCoseSign1Sig(
   258	  coseSign1: any,
   259	  leaf: Uint8Array,
   260	): Promise<void> {
   261	  const [protectedHeaders, , payload, signature] = coseSign1;
   262	  const tbs = new Uint8Array(
   263	    CBOR.encode([
   264	      "Signature1",
   265	      new Uint8Array(protectedHeaders),
   266	      new Uint8Array(0),
   267	      new Uint8Array(payload),
   268	    ]),
   269	  );
   270	
   271	  const leafCert = new x509.X509Certificate(leaf);
   272	  const pubKey = await importEcdsaPublicKey(leafCert.publicKey.rawData);
   273	
   274	  const cryptoInstance = await getCryptoInstance();
   275	  const ok = await cryptoInstance.subtle.verify(
   276	    { name: "ECDSA", hash: { name: "SHA-384" } },
   277	    pubKey,
   278	    new Uint8Array(signature),
   279	    tbs,
   280	  );
   281	  if (!ok) throw new Error("COSE_Sign1 ES384 verification failed");
   282	}
   283	
   284	function bytesEq(a: ArrayBuffer, b: ArrayBuffer) {
   285	  const A = new Uint8Array(a),
   286	    B = new Uint8Array(b);
   287	  if (A.length !== B.length) return false;
   288	  for (let i = 0; i < A.length; i++) if (A[i] !== B[i]) return false;
   289	  return true;
   290	}

     1	# Turnkey upstream source pins
     2	
     3	The C# port targets the **peak-pinned** Turnkey npm versions, NOT the Unity
     4	port's newer versions. The npm tarball contents (extracted under
     5	[`upstream-snapshots/`](./upstream-snapshots/)) are the authoritative source.
     6	GitHub SHAs are secondary metadata.
     7	
     8	## Pin table
     9	
    10	| src C# file                | Upstream snapshot path                  | npm package                | Version | Tarball sha256 |
    11	|---|---|---|---|---|
    12	| src/Encoding.cs            | turnkey-encoding-0.6.0                  | @turnkey/encoding          | 0.6.0   | `2cf9e6ee1f47ac7e3cc3e644cdb0e3e112c906a6ea1af737777f4658b73fb7bc` |
    13	| src/CryptoConstants.cs     | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `75115706fccc29c664f9f918d9a0c2c1798eb03f261cb5b0c186c75663cf79d3` |
    14	| src/Crypto.cs              | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `75115706fccc29c664f9f918d9a0c2c1798eb03f261cb5b0c186c75663cf79d3` |
    15	| src/ApiKeyStamper.cs       | turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0           | @turnkey/api-key-stamper   | 0.5.0   | `962a2d22c7c40240f05be98533769b37ab7dad7dbb5abec762c41007233d02bd` |
    16	| src/Http.cs                | turnkey-http-3.16.0                     | @turnkey/http              | 3.16.0  | `d849f2156633f63062c52067785df1ce33eac0659044df932862c5d6de9dbdaf` |
    17	| src/TurnkeyJsonContext.cs  | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | (no single upstream; covers DTOs from crypto + api-key-stamper + http) | n/a | n/a |
    18	
    19	Each upstream snapshot directory contains:
    20	
    21	- `package/` — verbatim npm tarball extract (the authoritative wire-format
    22	  source: `dist/*.js` + `dist/*.d.ts` + `package.json` + LICENSE / README).
    23	- `ts-source/` — the original TypeScript source from `github.com/tkhq/sdk` at
    24	  the matching git tag SHA (committed for human readability; the npm tarball
    25	  remains the wire-format source of truth if the two ever disagree).
    26	
    27	## Why these versions
    28	
    29	These are exactly what the peak monorepo pulls. See
    30	[`peak-lockfile-evidence.md`](./peak-lockfile-evidence.md) for the
    31	`pnpm-lock.yaml` lines.
    32	
    33	## GitHub commit SHAs (secondary)
    34	
    35	`gitHead` is **NOT present** in the published tarballs for these versions
    36	(`grep gitHead package/package.json` returns nothing for any of the four).
    37	The GitHub commit SHAs below are resolved from the git tag of the form
    38	`@turnkey/<pkg>@<version>` via `gh api /repos/tkhq/sdk/git/ref/tags/...`.
    39	These are recorded for cross-reference only. The npm tarball sha256 above
    40	is the controlling wire-format source.
    41	
    42	| npm package                | Version | Git tag SHA                                  | Reference URL |
    43	|---|---|---|---|

    45	| @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `b35dc642bd7c1728f97acd43d4cba66976b65084`   | https://github.com/tkhq/sdk/tree/b35dc642bd7c1728f97acd43d4cba66976b65084/packages/crypto |

    48	
    49	## Re-pinning procedure
    50	
    51	When bumping any pin:
    52	
    53	1. Update the table above (npm version, refresh tarball sha256, gitHead).
    54	2. Update `Directory.Packages.props` or any version comment.
    55	3. Re-run `npm pack` and refresh the extracted directories under
    56	   `upstream-snapshots/`.
    57	4. Re-run **3 Codex review rounds per affected file** via
    58	   [`codex-crypto-review.sh`](./codex-crypto-review.sh).
    59	5. Update `CHANGELOG.md`.

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/tink/elliptic_curves.ts | sed -n '1,220p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * Code modified from https://github.com/google/tink/blob/6f74b99a2bfe6677e3670799116a57268fd067fa/javascript/subtle/elliptic_curves.ts
     3	 * - The implementation of integerToByteArray has been modified to augment the resulting byte array to a certain length.
     4	 * - The implementation of PointDecode has been modified to decode both compressed and uncompressed points by checking for correct format
     5	 * - Method isP256CurvePoint added to check whether an uncompressed point is valid
     6	 *
     7	 * @license
     8	 * Copyright 2020 Google LLC
     9	 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
    10	 */
    11	
    12	import * as Bytes from "./bytes";
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * P-256 only
    16	 */
    17	function getModulus(): bigint {
    18	  // https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/FIPS/NIST.FIPS.186-4.pdf (Appendix D).
    19	  return BigInt(
    20	    "115792089210356248762697446949407573530086143415290314195533631308" +
    21	      "867097853951",
    22	  );
    23	}
    24	
    25	/**
    26	 * P-256 only
    27	 */
    28	function getB(): bigint {
    29	  // https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/FIPS/NIST.FIPS.186-4.pdf (Appendix D).
    30	  return BigInt(
    31	    "0x5ac635d8aa3a93e7b3ebbd55769886bc651d06b0cc53b0f63bce3c3e27d2604b",
    32	  );
    33	}
    34	
    35	/** Converts byte array to bigint. */
    36	function byteArrayToInteger(bytes: Uint8Array): bigint {
    37	  return BigInt("0x" + Bytes.toHex(bytes));
    38	}
    39	
    40	/** Converts bigint to byte array. */
    41	function integerToByteArray(i: bigint, length: number): Uint8Array {
    42	  const input = i.toString(16);
    43	  const numHexChars = length * 2;
    44	  let padding = "";
    45	  if (numHexChars < input.length) {
    46	    throw new Error(
    47	      `cannot pack integer with ${input.length} hex chars into ${length} bytes`,
    48	    );
    49	  } else {
    50	    padding = "0".repeat(numHexChars - input.length);
    51	  }
    52	  return Bytes.fromHex(padding + input);
    53	}
    54	
    55	/** Returns true iff the ith bit (in lsb order) of n is set. */
    56	function testBit(n: bigint, i: number): boolean {
    57	  const m = BigInt(1) << BigInt(i);
    58	  return (n & m) !== BigInt(0);
    59	}
    60	
    61	/**
    62	 * Computes a modular exponent.  Since JavaScript BigInt operations are not
    63	 * constant-time, information about the inputs could leak.  Therefore, THIS
    64	 * METHOD SHOULD ONLY BE USED FOR POINT DECOMPRESSION.
    65	 *
    66	 * @param b base
    67	 * @param exp exponent
    68	 * @param p modulus
    69	 * @return b^exp modulo p
    70	 */
    71	function modPow(b: bigint, exp: bigint, p: bigint): bigint {
    72	  if (exp === BigInt(0)) {
    73	    return BigInt(1);
    74	  }
    75	  let result = b;
    76	  const exponentBitString = exp.toString(2);
    77	  for (let i = 1; i < exponentBitString.length; ++i) {
    78	    result = (result * result) % p;
    79	    if (exponentBitString[i] === "1") {
    80	      result = (result * b) % p;
    81	    }
    82	  }
    83	  return result;
    84	}
    85	
    86	/**
    87	 * Computes a square root modulo an odd prime.  Since timing and exceptions can
    88	 * leak information about the inputs, THIS METHOD SHOULD ONLY BE USED FOR
    89	 * POINT DECOMPRESSION.
    90	 *
    91	 * @param x square
    92	 * @param p prime modulus
    93	 * @return square root of x modulo p
    94	 */
    95	function modSqrt(x: bigint, p: bigint): bigint {
    96	  if (p <= BigInt(0)) {
    97	    throw new Error("p must be positive");
    98	  }
    99	  const base = x % p;
   100	  // The currently supported NIST curves P-256, P-384, and P-521 all satisfy
   101	  // p % 4 == 3.  However, although currently a no-op, the following check
   102	  // should be left in place in case other curves are supported in the future.
   103	  if (testBit(p, 0) && /* istanbul ignore next */ testBit(p, 1)) {
   104	    // Case p % 4 == 3 (applies to NIST curves P-256, P-384, and P-521)
   105	    // q = (p + 1) / 4
   106	    const q = (p + BigInt(1)) >> BigInt(2);
   107	    const squareRoot = modPow(base, q, p);
   108	    if ((squareRoot * squareRoot) % p !== base) {
   109	      throw new Error("could not find a modular square root");
   110	    }
   111	    return squareRoot;
   112	  }
   113	  // Skipping other elliptic curve types that require Cipolla's algorithm.
   114	  throw new Error("unsupported modulus value");
   115	}
   116	
   117	/**
   118	 * Computes the y-coordinate of a point on an elliptic curve given its
   119	 * x-coordinate.  Since timing and exceptions can leak information about the
   120	 * inputs, THIS METHOD SHOULD ONLY BE USED FOR POINT DECOMPRESSION.
   121	 *
   122	 * P-256 only
   123	 *
   124	 * @param x x-coordinate
   125	 * @param lsb least significant bit of the y-coordinate
   126	 * @return y-coordinate
   127	 */
   128	function getY(x: bigint, lsb: boolean): bigint {
   129	  const p = getModulus();
   130	  const a = p - BigInt(3);
   131	  const b = getB();
   132	  const rhs = ((x * x + a) * x + b) % p;
   133	  let y = modSqrt(rhs, p);
   134	  if (lsb !== testBit(y, 0)) {
   135	    y = (p - y) % p;
   136	  }
   137	  return y;
   138	}
   139	
   140	/**
   141	 *
   142	 * Given x and y coordinates of a JWK, checks whether these are valid points on
   143	 * the P-256 elliptic curve.
   144	 *
   145	 * P-256 only
   146	 *
   147	 * @param x x-coordinate
   148	 * @param y y-coordinate
   149	 * @return boolean validity
   150	 */
   151	function isP256CurvePoint(x: bigint, y: bigint): boolean {
   152	  const p = getModulus();
   153	  const a = p - BigInt(3);
   154	  const b = getB();
   155	  const rhs = ((x * x + a) * x + b) % p;
   156	  const lhs = y ** BigInt(2) % p;
   157	  return lhs === rhs;
   158	}
   159	
   160	/**
   161	 * Decodes a public key in _compressed_ OR _uncompressed_ format.
   162	 * Augmented to ensure that the x and y components are padded to fit 32 bytes.
   163	 *
   164	 * P-256 only
   165	 */
   166	export function pointDecode(point: Uint8Array): JsonWebKey {
   167	  const fieldSize = fieldSizeInBytes();
   168	  const compressedLength = fieldSize + 1;
   169	  const uncompressedLength = 2 * fieldSize + 1;
   170	  if (
   171	    point.length !== compressedLength &&
   172	    point.length !== uncompressedLength
   173	  ) {
   174	    throw new Error(
   175	      "Invalid length: point is not in compressed or uncompressed format",
   176	    );
   177	  }
   178	  // Decodes point if its length and first bit match the compressed format
   179	  if ((point[0] === 2 || point[0] === 3) && point.length == compressedLength) {
   180	    const lsb = point[0] === 3; // point[0] must be 2 (false) or 3 (true).
   181	    const x = byteArrayToInteger(point.subarray(1, point.length));
   182	    const p = getModulus();
   183	    if (x < BigInt(0) || x >= p) {
   184	      throw new Error("x is out of range");
   185	    }
   186	    const y = getY(x, lsb);
   187	    const result: JsonWebKey = {
   188	      kty: "EC",
   189	      crv: "P-256",
   190	      x: Bytes.toBase64(integerToByteArray(x, 32), /* websafe */ true),
   191	      y: Bytes.toBase64(integerToByteArray(y, 32), /* websafe */ true),
   192	      ext: true,
   193	    };
   194	    return result;
   195	    // Decodes point if its length and first bit match the uncompressed format
   196	  } else if (point[0] === 4 && point.length == uncompressedLength) {
   197	    const x = byteArrayToInteger(point.subarray(1, fieldSize + 1));
   198	    const y = byteArrayToInteger(
   199	      point.subarray(fieldSize + 1, 2 * fieldSize + 1),
   200	    );
   201	    const p = getModulus();
   202	    if (
   203	      x < BigInt(0) ||
   204	      x >= p ||
   205	      y < BigInt(0) ||
   206	      y >= p ||
   207	      !isP256CurvePoint(x, y)
   208	    ) {
   209	      throw new Error("invalid uncompressed x and y coordinates");
   210	    }
   211	    const result: JsonWebKey = {
   212	      kty: "EC",
   213	      crv: "P-256",
   214	      x: Bytes.toBase64(integerToByteArray(x, 32), /* websafe */ true),
   215	      y: Bytes.toBase64(integerToByteArray(y, 32), /* websafe */ true),
   216	      ext: true,
   217	    };
   218	    return result;
   219	  }
   220	  throw new Error("invalid format");

    62	
    63	// Convert base64 url encoded string to an array -- used here to test that output pads correctly and doesn't get truncated
    64	function base64urlToBuffer(baseurl64String: string): ArrayBuffer {
    65	  // Base64url to Base64
    66	  const padding = "==".slice(0, (4 - (baseurl64String.length % 4)) % 4);
    67	  const base64String =
    68	    baseurl64String.replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/") + padding;
    69	
    70	  // Base64 to binary string
    71	  const str = atob(base64String);
    72	
    73	  // Binary string to buffer
    74	  const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(str.length);
    75	  const byteView = new Uint8Array(buffer);
    76	  for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
    77	    byteView[i] = str.charCodeAt(i);
    78	  }
    79	  return buffer;
    80	}

**C. Cryptographic Claims**

No cryptographic correction proposed.

- HPKE/QOS: current v3 no longer claims SDK HPKE is QOS or non-RFC. Pinned `crypto.ts` has `hpkeEncrypt` / `hpkeAuthEncrypt` JSdoc referencing RFC 9180 and uses generated P-256 sender keys, HKDF-SHA256, AES-GCM, and compressed sender output at `upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts:87-152` and `:154-216`. QOS is separate: `quorumKeyEncrypt` cites QOS, uses nonce, borsh, SHA-512 HMAC-derived AES-GCM key at `:218-276` and `:791-856`.
- Suite IDs/labels: constants match plan claims at `upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/constants.ts:1-23`; C# constants mirror them at `src/Crypto.cs:76-108`.
- Noble deterministic low-S: `purejs.ts` hashes content then calls `p256.sign(hash, privateKey)` and DER-encodes at `upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/purejs.ts:21-23`; package dependency is `@noble/curves:^1.3.0` at `package/package.json:50-53`. This is load-bearing for Tier-2 exact DER snapshots, and the plan’s lockfile + preflight check is the right guard.
- Stamper JSON order/scheme: `index.ts` creates `{ publicKey, scheme, signature }`, with `SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256`, then `JSON.stringify`s it at `upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/index.ts:94-103`. Upstream test asserts key order and scheme at `__tests__/stamp-test.ts:24-32`.
- Tarballs omit tests/fixtures: package `files` only include `dist/`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `README.md` for stamper, crypto, and http at package.json lines `36-40`, `30-34`, `33-37`; no extracted `package/__tests__` or `package/__fixtures__` directories exist.
